Mindmap structure (mirrors Shopee PDF): (1) Trigger A — Failed Delivery: 3 sub-states (Returning to seller / Delivered back / Lost in transit) → WH inspect within 2 WD → 3 outcomes (Resellable / Damaged / Empty) → dispute path with 1st/2nd Reimbursement Coverage rounds. (2) Trigger B — Buyer R/R Request: Refund Only vs Return+Refund flows → 1st/2nd/3rd 24h SLA windows → approve/reject decisions → dispute path. (3) SLA Windows critical reference: 1st 24h / 2nd 24h / 3rd 24h / Speedy Refund 1 WD / 1-month appeal / Reimbursement Coverage filing. (4) 2nd Dispute via Ticket Log: TT Help Center navigation + Order ID filter + Latest Message verdict reading. (5) Internal System Logging: same-day rule + webapp action states (WH Evidence/CS Submission/CS Follow Up/Closed) + refund_state values + remarks discipline. (6) Critical Rules / Anti-Patterns: never redirect buyer to TT CS (RM 1,494.49 lost C1371+C1473), Speedy Refund 1 WD only, 2nd 24h window applies AFTER buyer ships, packing VIDEO required (not photos), same-day webapp logging, WH inspect 2 WD, Order ID not case ID, resell needs WH inspection first. (7) Closure Outcomes glossary: LOSS / IN DISPUTE / RESELL/WITHDRAWN / PENDING REOPEN / IN TRANSIT / TT CLOSED / CREDITED / NOT IN INTERNAL. (Bonus 1) CS Daily Routine: morning/throughout-day/afternoon/evening cadence. (Bonus 2) Webapp PATCH cheatsheet: refund_state Credited/Rejected/Withdrawn body + remark body + TT-vs-Shopee endpoint warning.
Shops affected: All 13 TT MY shops (training material, not shop data). Adelmar / Dasnature / Hiranai / Hiranai MY / Jager / JagerArmor / JagerSafety / KarlMobel / Lovento / MurahYa / ValueSnap / DasNature 2 / and any future TT shop added.
